ARCOMMANDS_Types.h
libARCommands types header. This file contains all types declarations needed to use commands ...
ARCOMMANDS_Generator_GenerateSkyControllerButtonMappingsStateAllCurrentButtonMappingsSent
eARCOMMANDS_GENERATOR_ERROR ARCOMMANDS_Generator_GenerateSkyControllerButtonMappingsStateAllCurrentButtonMappingsSent(uint8_t *buffer, int32_t buffLen, int32_t *cmdLen)
Sent by the SkyController to notify the end of a currentButtonMappings events list. If the list is empty (e.g. the controller sent a setButtonMapping command which made no change to the mapping table), then this command will be sent without any currentButtonMappings event preceding it. This gives the controller a reliable synchronization point when editing mappings.
